## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
  participant Runner
  participant Main
  participant Simulate
  participant DrawETA as draw_sample_eta
  participant DrawRollup as draw_rollup_sample
  participant GetStats as get_model_stats
  participant File
  participant DrawHierarchy as draw_sample_hierarchy
  participant Mapper as common_model_mapper
  participant ML as common_ml_algorithm

  Runner->>Main: call main()
  Main->>Simulate: invoke simulate()
  Simulate->>DrawETA: draw_sample_eta()
  DrawETA->>DrawRollup: draw_rollup_sample()
  DrawRollup->>GetStats: get_model_stats()
  GetStats->>File: open/read model_stats.json
  File-->>GetStats: return JSON
  GetStats-->>DrawRollup: return stats
  DrawRollup-->>DrawETA: return rollup sample
  DrawETA-->>Simulate: return eta
  Simulate->>DrawHierarchy: draw_sample_hierarchy()
  DrawHierarchy->>Mapper: access MODEL_HIERARCHY & enums
  Mapper-->>DrawHierarchy: return models
  DrawHierarchy-->>Simulate: return hierarchy
  Simulate->>ML: get_default_algorithm(model_type_name)
  ML-->>Simulate: return algorithm dict
  loop algorithm steps
    Simulate->>Simulate: compute predicted_eta & conf
    Simulate-->>Simulate: print results / accept or continue
  end
  Simulate-->>Main: done
  Main-->>Runner: exit
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram
  [*] --> Idle
  Idle --> Sampling_Rollup
  Sampling_Rollup --> Sampling_ETA
  Sampling_ETA --> Sampling_Hierarchy
  Sampling_Hierarchy --> Evaluating
  Evaluating --> Accepted: conf >= threshold && conditions met
  Evaluating --> Evaluating: next algorithm step
  Evaluating --> [*]: finished
```
